 saamne aae maamalon main kis tarah sakht se sakht karrwai kii ja sake
 It has been informed by the government that an Electronic Compliant Box has been formed by the Ministry of Women and Child Development, in which women can file their complaints
 ek baar jab shikaayat is SHE BOX main chali jaaegi, tab sidhe taur par ye shikaayat athurity ke paas jaaegi
 Significantly, under the # metoo campaign, there have been many cases of sexual abuse against women at workplaces
 iske kaaran desh kii raajnneeti or film industry main bhuuchaal aa gaya he
 Minister of State for External Affairs MJ Akbar faced many charges under this campaign, after which he had to resign from his post
 pehle diya tha cameti banane ke prastaavbata den ki isse pehle bhi kendriya mahila evam bal vikaas mantralay ne aise maamalon kii jaanch ke liye ek cameti gathit karne kaa elaan kiya tha, haalanki baad main isamen badlaav kiya gaya
 The letter was also written to political parties: Union Women Development Minister Maneka Gandhi wrote a letter to political parties on this issue
 is chitthee main unhone sabhi raajnneetik dalon ke adhyakshon / kaaryakari adhyakshon se apil kii thi ki vah apni party meninternal cametika gathan karen

 ye cameti 2013 ke sexual herracement act ke tahat banaai jaaegi
 Maneka Gandhi has requested political parties to form such a committee at national and state levels

 bharat main rkyrat royal bank of scotland (RBS India) ne apane karmchaariyon ke saim sex partner ke liye bhi swasthya beemaa kaa cover muhaiyaa karaane kaa nirnay liya he
 This can be called a bold decision, because gay couples or homosexuality still do not have legal status in India
 vaise is kadam ke kanoonee pachade main bhi funsane kii ashanka he
 Same sex partner means that if someone is gay or lesbian, they can also add their partner to their health insurance benefits
 abhi tak bhartiya corporate jagat main karmchaariyon ko jo swasthya beemaa yojana muhaiyaa kii jaati he, usamen unke pati-patni, bachche, maa-baap yaa saas-sasur ko shaamil kiya jaataa he
 According to the news of Times of India, Homo sexuality, lesbian, gay, bisexual or trans gender sex is considered a crime under Section 377 in India
 isliye aise kisi bhi partner ko kisi bhi tarah kii beemaa yojana main shaamil nahin kiya jaataa
 Hence RBS decided that it would bear the cost of providing insurance facility to the same sex partner
 haalanki, yah sochane vaali baat he ki agar aise sexl relation yapartner rakhanagaiyr kanoonee he to phir yah bank is tarah ke partner ko beemaa cover kaise de saktaa he
 Therefore it seems that this facility may also get caught in the legal trouble
 bank main yah niti nae vitt varsh yani 1 april se lagu ho jaaegi
 Till now companies have been providing all kinds of facilities to their employees, but this facility has come up for the first time
 kai companiyon main is par charchaa jarur thi ki saim sex partner ko bhi beemaa suvidha milani chahie, lekin isaki shuruyaat koi kar nahin paaya tha
 However, many companies had introduced facilities like Adoption Leave, Paternity Leave, Relocation for same sex partner
 haalanki companiyon ke saamne yah chunauti rahi he ki kis tarah se bhartiya kanoon ke daayre main rah kar yah sab kiya jaae, kyonki bharat main saim sex shaadi ko abhi vaid nahin mana gaya he
 The Supreme Court has given freedom to express sexual orientation, but has not reversed the law that makes sex relations a crime
 haalanki supreme court ne kaha he ki vah dhara 377 kaa punarpareekshan karegaa
